                    ""PRIOR_VAX"": ""IPV""
                }
            }, {
                ""range"": {
                    ""RECVDATE"": {
                        ""gte"": ""2018-01-01"",
                        ""lte"": ""2019-01-01""
                    }
                }
            }]
        }
    }
}
```
